Device Usage Page (device_usage_statistics.html)

This HTML page displays the device usage statistics that will be sent to Xilinx. The file also contains predefined XML tags used to simplify processing.
 
Please verify the contents are okay to send to Xilinx!

Tool Usage
Command Line History
  • xst -intstyle ise -ifn <fname>.xst -ofn <fname>.syr
  • ngdbuild -intstyle ise -dd <ise_file> -nt timestamp -uc <fname>.ucf -p xc2v1000-fg456-4 <fname>.ngc <fname>.ngd
  • map -intstyle ise -p xc2v1000-fg456-4 -timing -ol med -t 1 -cm area -pr b -k 4 -c 100 -tx off -o <fname>.ncd <fname>.ngd <fname>.pcf
  • par -w -intstyle ise -ol med -t 1 <fname>.ncd <fname>.ncd <fname>.pcf
  • trce -intstyle ise -e 3 -l 3 -s 4 -xml top <fname>.ncd -o <fname>.twr <fname>.pcf
  • bitgen -intstyle ise -f <fname>.ut <fname>.ncd
